### [93] [Visual Instruction Tuning Aligns Modalities through Abstraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03871)
*Luis Palacios,Lorenzo Basile,Diego Doimo,Alberto Cazzaniga*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究了视觉指令微调在LLM中的作用，发现其主要将视觉特征直接嵌入LLM的中间语义层，而非早期层；中间层是多模态表征与任务性能的关键。通过探针与因果干预验证，并显示只微调中间层即可接近全量微调的效果、节省训练时间。结论：多模态整合是局部化地复用LLM内部抽象引擎。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 跨多种视觉-语言架构进行：1) 层级探针分析，观察不同层对视觉语义的编码；2) 因果干预（如遮蔽、打乱或重置特定层/通道）评估层的重要性；3) 表征几何比较，衡量语义等价的图像与文本在向量空间的一致性；4) 局部微调实验，仅在中间层进行微调并评估基准性能与训练成本。

Result: 发现视觉特征主要在中间语义层被注入和对齐，早期层仍偏向单模态处理；中间层对多种多模态基准性能至关重要。微调加强了中间层现有抽象阶段，并使视觉表示与原有文本表示对齐。仅微调中间层在视觉中心任务上能保持接近全量微调的表现，同时显著降低训练时间。

Conclusion: 多模态整合并非全网络均匀发生，而是集中在LLM的中间语义层，通过复用其内部抽象机制实现。实践上，聚焦中间层进行局部微调可在性能与效率间取得良好权衡，并为设计更轻量的多模态适配方案提供依据。

Abstract: Visual instruction tuning effectively adapts a pre-trained Large Language Model (LLM) to process image information alongside text. Yet, it remains unclear how visual features are embedded into the layer-wise hierarchy of abstractions of the LLM backbone. Across a diverse set of vision-language architectures, we show that instruction tuning primarily serves as a bridge, embedding visual features directly into the intermediate semantic layers of the LLM, bypassing the early layers devoted to unimodal processing. With probing analyses and causal interventions, we show that these intermediate layers are the semantic core of vision-language processing and play a critical role in the performance on a broad set of multimodal benchmarks. In addition, by comparing the geometry of semantically equivalent visual and textual representations, we find that fine-tuning extends and strengthens the existing abstraction phase, aligning visual features with pre-existing textual ones. Finally, we confirm the functional role of this localized alignment by restricting fine-tuning to intermediate layers alone: this strategy preserves the performance of full fine-tuning on vision-centric benchmarks while reducing training time. Our results suggest that multimodal integration is a localized phenomenon driven by the repurposing of the internal abstraction engine of the LLM.

Abstract: We present DyaPlex, a streaming, full-duplex speech-and-motion model designed for dyadic interaction. At its core, our method leverages the strong priors of a foundational full-duplex speech model and integrates a novel motion pathway, thereby achieving fully synchronized multi-modal interaction. ### [95] [Seg2Track++: Probabilistic Track Validation and Data Association for Multi-Object Tracking and Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03875)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在SAM2实例分割基础上，提出Seg2Track++的跟踪管理：1) 轨迹关联：利用掩码质心距离（MCD）度量空间一致性，并用置信感知代价调制（CCM）结合分割置信度调整关联代价；2) 概率化轨迹验证（PTV）：用伯努利滤波对轨迹存在性建模，动态确认/终止轨迹以抑制幽灵轨迹；整体实现零样本MOTS的时序一致分割与跟踪。

Conclusion: 通过把强零样本分割与专门的关联与存在性验证模块耦合，Seg2Track++在无需训练的情况下显著提升MOTS性能，适合自动系统在动态环境中的稳健感知。

Foundation models such as SAM2 have shown strong zero-shot generalization for segmentation, but their direct application to MOTS is limited by unreliable track association and false-positive propagation. This work introduces Seg2Track++, a framework that integrates instance segmentation with SAM2 and a novel track management module to perform zero-shot MOTS with enhanced temporal consistency. Tracks are associated using Mask Centroid Distance (MCD) and Confidence-Aware Cost Modulation (CCM), while Probabilistic Track Validation (PTV) employs a Bernoulli filter to validate track existence and suppress ghost tracks. Experimental results on KITTI MOTS demonstrate improved identity preservation, reduced false-positive propagation, and robust track management without fine-tuning.

### [96] [MLP Splatting: Object-Centric Neural Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03877)
*Shinjeong Kim,Yuzhou Cheng,Xin Kong,Paul H. J. Kelly,Andrew J. Davison*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MLP-Splatting：用少量、可分解的轻量神经光场原语实现照片级新视角合成与可编辑场景表示。每个原语是局部支持的紧凑MLP，进行稀疏体渲染；仅用RGB监督即可学到对象/部件级原语，并可选蒸馏语义特征以支持开放词汇交互与即刻分割。相较语义3DGS，内存降至1/15、渲染提速约3×。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3DGS与NeRF虽能高质合成，但难以将场景直接分解为少量可控的对象级原语，需额外分割/聚类；而单一全局辐射场或低级高斯原语在表达性与可局部编辑之间权衡不佳。需要一种既具高表达能力、又天然可分解与可编辑的场景表示。

Method: 以“原语”为基本单元：每个原语是具有局部空间支持的紧凑MLP，预测该局部的辐射与不透明度。渲染通过光线与原语交互的稀疏体合成完成。训练仅用多视角RGB监督；可选地蒸馏语义特征，使原语带有开放词汇对齐。通过选择少量原语即可进行对象级交互和编辑。

Result: 在与语义3DGS等SOTA比较中，实现显著更低资源与更高速度：约1/15的内存占用、约3×的渲染速度，同时保持照片级新视角质量；原语往往与对象/部件对齐，支持无需掩码的交互式编辑，并在蒸馏后实现开放词汇交互与开集即刻分割。

Conclusion: MLP-Splatting以局部神经原语替代高斯或全局场，实现可分解、可编辑且高效的3D表示，在保持合成质量的同时显著降低内存并加速渲染，并扩展到开放词汇场景理解与交互。

Abstract: 3D representations are fundamental to scene rendering, understanding, and interaction. Recent approaches, such as 3D Gaussian Splatting and Neural Radiance Fields, achieve impressive photorealistic novel-view synthesis, but lack the ability to easily decompose scene elements into a few primitives, requiring additional segmentation or grouping for object-level manipulation. We present MLP-Splatting, a method that enables scene decomposition via a few expressive light-field primitives while providing photorealistic novel-view synthesis.
  MLP-Splatting models each primitive as an independent compact MLP with localized spatial support that predicts radiance and opacity. In contrast to low-level Gaussian primitives or a single global radiance field, our neural primitives provide greater expressive capacity while remaining spatially localized. Rendering is performed through efficient sparse volumetric compositing over ray-primitive interactions.
  Our primitives are supervised using RGB supervision alone, which yields primitives that represent local scene regions often corresponding to objects or object parts, enabling interactive object-level editing without segmentation masks by selecting a handful of primitives. Our method, augmented with optional semantic feature distillation, enables open-vocabulary scene interaction and open-set instant segmentation. Compared to state-of-the-art methods, we achieve substantially lower memory usage (1/15$\times$) and faster rendering (3$\times$), as we show in our experiments compared to semantic 3DGS methods. Project Page: https://shinjeongkim.com/mlp-splatting

</details>


### [97] [Beyond Encoder Accumulation: Measuring Encoder Roles in Multi-Encoder VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03879)
*Wei Ding,Yudong Zhang,Ruobing Xie,Xingwu Sun,Jiansheng Chen,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文系统研究多编码器LVLM在联合训练中的交互：对5个常见视觉编码器的31个非空子集进行统一重训与评测，提出“能力-必要性”分解与投影前有效秩分析，给出小而强的编码器组合准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LVLM融合更多异构视觉流，如何在联合训练下理解不同视觉编码器的作用与交互、并在训练前找到参数高效的配置仍缺乏体系化方法。现有通过在固定检查点上“遮蔽”编码器来评估贡献的做法可能产生误判。

Method: 在Cambrian-1包含16个基准上，统一管线重训并评估由5个常见视觉编码器构成的31个非空子集（约2万GPU小时）。提出两种分析：1）能力（单独使用该编码器的得分）与必要性（从完整五编码器模型移除该编码器导致的分数下降）；2）在固定参数预算下，分析各编码器“预投影层”输出的有效秩，考察其在联合训练中的保留或扩展。

Result: 1）从零重训得到的编码器排序与在固定检查点上遮蔽得到的排序显著不同，甚至第一名编码器都改变。2）能力与必要性不等价；将两个最高能力编码器配对次优，而“高能力锚点+自适应互补”的二元组合可匹敌五编码器模型；再加入更多编码器收益边际很小。3）在相同参数量下，解释剩余性能差异的关键是每个编码器预投影器的有效秩：最强组合由一个在联合训练下保持高秩的锚点与一个能在此条件下扩展秩的互补组成。

Conclusion: 遮蔽法存在方法学偏差；应采用重训与“能力-必要性”分解，并结合预投影有效秩作为设计原语。实践上，优选“高能力且秩可保留”的锚点+“可在该锚点下扩展秩”的互补二元组合，在参数受限时接近多编码器上限，额外编码器仅带来微弱增益。

Abstract: As foundation models scale toward fusing more heterogeneous visual streams, understanding how diverse encoders interact under joint training becomes a prerequisite for principled design. Yet large vision-language models (LVLMs) currently lack the tools to do so, and parameter-efficient encoder configurations remain hard to identify before training. To re-examine encoder roles under joint training, on the 16-benchmark Cambrian-1 suite we retrain and evaluate all 31 non-empty subsets of five common vision encoders under a unified pipeline (~20k GPU-hours total), and report three findings. First, retraining each subset from scratch reveals encoder rankings that differ from those obtained by masking encoders on a fixed checkpoint, including which encoder ranks first overall. Second, we decompose each encoder's contribution into two axes, Capacity, the score an encoder reaches on its own, and Necessity, the drop when it is removed from the full pool. The two axes are not interchangeable. Pairing the two highest-Capacity encoders is suboptimal, while pairing a high-Capacity anchor with an adaptive complement matches the full five-encoder model. Adding further encoders beyond this pair yields only marginal gains. Third, at fixed parameter count, per-encoder pre-projector effective rank explains the residual score variation. The strongest pairs combine an anchor whose rank survives joint training with a complement whose rank expands under it, suggesting that higher-rank, less-collapsed projector inputs correspond to a more favorable optimization regime at the encoder-projector interface. Together, the Capacity-Necessity decomposition and the pre-projector rank analysis, along with comprehensive evaluation through retraining, expose a methodological gap in multi-encoder LVLM design, and offer concrete primitives for closing it.

</details>

Method: 扩展DINO到3D：采用分层3D Swin作为骨干；对来自多尺度层级的特征进行拼接后实施自蒸馏（teacher-student），从而同时编码全局语义与细粒度局部结构；强调数据效率与无标注预训练流程。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning has enabled large-scale pre-training on 2D natural images, producing general-purpose visual representations that transfer effectively across tasks. However, many medical imaging modalities, such as CT scans, are inherently three-dimensional and differ fundamentally from natural images in both structure and semantics. Volumetric modalities capture spatial continuity, organ anatomy, and intensity-based tissue properties (e.g., Hounsfield Units), which are not adequately modeled by 2D pre-training. To bridge this gap, we introduce CoralBay, a self-distillation framework that extends DINO by using a hierarchical 3D Swin backbone and applying self-distillation to concatenated multi-scale features, enabling data-efficient self-supervised learning of rich spatial representations that encode both global semantics and fine-grained local structure. As a result, CoralBay transfers effectively to a wide range of downstream radiological tasks, demonstrating strong and consistent performance across diverse anatomical targets. In addition, we contribute to the open-source \eva framework by introducing a public, reproducible 3D radiology leaderboard that unifies multiple datasets and establishes a standardized benchmark for evaluating volumetric representation learning methods.

*Yifei Li,Pengyiang Liu,Yuhang Zang,Zhongyue Shi,Qi Fu,Hongye Hao,Jiwen Lu*

Result: 人类专家86.6分，最佳模型Gemini-3.1-Pro为59.2，落后27分。主要瓶颈在allocentric mapping。意外发现：为流式/空间任务专项微调的MLLM反而不如其基座；缺乏视频证据支撑的链式思维会放大空间性错误。

Conclusion: OVO-S-Bench揭示现有MLLM在流式空间推理上的显著不足，尤其在视角转换与全局地图构建。该基准为下一代流式空间多模态模型提供了严格而针对性的测试平台，并提示训练与推理需更注重证据对齐与空间一致性。

Abstract: Multimodal agents in robotics, AR, and autonomous driving must reason about places and layouts from continuous egocentric streams, often using evidence outside the current view. Existing benchmarks either evaluate offline over full videos or target events rather than spatial structure. We introduce OVO-S-Bench, a fully human-annotated benchmark for streaming spatial intelligence, comprising 1,680 questions over 348 source videos. Annotation involves 12 trained annotators, each also serving as a blind cross-reviewer, across roughly 804 person-hours of multi-round quality assurance. Each question carries a query timestamp and an evidence interval, and at evaluation, the model sees only the prefix preceding the query. Questions span four levels of increasing abstraction: instantaneous egocentric perception, spatiotemporal context tracking, spatial simulation and reasoning, and allocentric mapping. Across 38 proprietary and open-source MLLMs, Gemini-3.1-Pro trails human experts by 27 points, 59.2 vs. 86.6, with allocentric mapping as the dominant bottleneck. Notably, streaming and spatially fine-tuned MLLMs underperform their own backbones. We further find that chain-of-thought reasoning amplifies spatial errors when ungrounded in the stream. By exposing these limitations, OVO-S-Bench establishes a demanding testbed for next-generation streaming spatial MLLMs.

### [100] [Electromagnetic Navigation for Femoral Osteotomy Using High-Accuracy X-ray-to-CT Registration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03893)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建集成导航流程：1) 依据CT进行术前三维规划；2) 术中一次性C臂标定；3) 仅用初始化阶段两张透视图完成高精度X线-CT配准；4) 借助EMT对锯片与骨段进行实时、免透视导航，适配单/双平面截骨。以18根仿骨开展可行性实验，对比自由手与PSI，评估角度与平移误差、超阈值率及用户问卷。

Conclusion: 该EMT导航系统用两张透视图即可把术前规划可靠转移到术中，匹配PSI精度且不增加手术暴露与辐射，显著优于自由手，具备推进尸体与临床验证的意义。

Abstract: Accurate execution of preoperative plans in corrective femoral osteotomies remains challenging. Current techniques are limited by variable accuracy, invasiveness, and radiation exposure, with free-hand methods and patient-specific instrumentation (PSI) often requiring >30 and >6 fluoroscopic images, respectively. We present an integrated, electromagnetic tracking (EMT)-based navigation system for femoral osteotomies that minimizes dissection and intraoperative fluoroscopy. The system couples CT-based preoperative planning with one-time intraoperative C-arm calibration and accurate X-ray-to-CT registration from two fluoroscopic images acquired at initialization. This enables real-time, fluoroscopy-free EMT navigation of the saw blade and bone fragments relative to the preoperative plan, and is compatible with uniplanar and biplanar osteotomies. In a feasibility study using 18 synthetic femora, EMT guidance significantly outperformed free-hand execution in total angular error ($(3.05 \pm 0.75)^\circ$ vs.\ $(6.32 \pm 2.36)^\circ$, $p=0.031$), assuming the same minimal surgical exposure for both. No EMT-guided trials exceeded the >5° clinical threshold, whereas free-hand produced 4 outliers of 6 trials. The system achieved statistical equivalence ($\pm 2^\circ$, $\pm 2,\text{mm}$) to PSI for total angular ($p \le 0.02$) and total translational ($p=0.048$) errors, with no significant differences in user questionnaire scores. By transferring preoperative plans using only two fluoroscopic images while matching PSI accuracy without additional surgical exposure, the proposed system motivates subsequent cadaveric and clinical validation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建噪声感知的注意力型去噪网络：1) 层级Swin Transformer窗口注意力进行上下文建模；2) 基于Transformer的多维门控细化模块进行通道自适应增强；3) 显式噪声水平条件输入与残差重建，实现对不同强度Rician噪声的自适应抑制与稳定恢复。

Abstract: Diffusion-weighted imaging (DWI) is used for whole-body cancer screening, but it typically requires a long acquisition time. When the scan time is reduced, the image quality often suffers, leading to increased noise in the scans. Magnitude reconstruction in DWI introduces signal-dependent Rician noise, which makes denoising more challenging for conventional convolution-based methods. To address this limitation, we propose a noise-aware attention-driven denoising framework that integrates hierarchical Swin Transformer window attention with transformer-based multi-dimensional gated refinement for DWI restoration. The model incorporates explicit noise-level conditioning and residual reconstruction to enable adaptive suppression of heteroscedastic noise across a wide range of corruption levels. Experimental evaluation on corrupted DWI scans demonstrates strong restoration performance. Our model achieves a mean PSNR of 33.69~dB and SSIM of 0.8539 across noise levels from 1\% to 15\%, while maintaining stable behavior under severe noise conditions. These results indicate that attention-guided contextual modeling combined with channel-adaptive refinement provides a robust and generalizable solution for DWI denoising.

### [102] [SparseStreet: Sparse Gaussian Splatting for Real-Time Street Scene Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03909)
*Qingpo Wuwu,Xiaobao Wei,Peng Chen,Nan Huang,Zhongyu Zhao,Hao Wang,Ming Lu,Ningning Ma,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SparseStreet：针对街景3D Gaussian Splatting的通用压缩框架，结合可学习节点级剪枝与背景压缩，优先保真动态目标，显著减少高斯原语数量，在Waymo/nuScenes上实现最高约80%压缩且几乎无质量损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 街景重建中3D Gaussian Splatting虽效果好，但需大量高斯原语以刻画细节，造成存储庞大与渲染缓慢；同时动态物体需高保真以保持时序一致，而静态背景存在大量冗余。因此需要一种在不牺牲关键动态区域质量的前提下，显著压缩场景表示的方案。

Method: 提出SparseStreet两阶段框架：1) 节点式可学习剪枝（node-based learnable pruning），依据贡献度系统性移除低贡献高斯原语，聚焦保留视觉关键区域与动态目标；2) 表示稳定后进行背景压缩（background compression），进一步减少静态区域冗余。总体目标是在保证动态对象几何与外观的同时压缩原语数量。

Result: 在Waymo与nuScenes数据集上，SparseStreet在保持动态物体几何与外观高保真的同时，大幅减少高斯原语数量，压缩率最高可达约80%，质量劣化极小，并实现资源高效、快速渲染的动态场景重建。

Conclusion: 面向街景的SparseStreet能在保证动态区域时序一致与视觉质量的前提下，通过可学习剪枝与背景压缩有效压缩3DGS表示，显著降低存储与提高渲染效率，适用于高保真动态街景重建。

Abstract: While 3D Gaussian Splatting has shown promising results in street scene reconstruction, existing methods require massive numbers of Gaussian primitives to capture fine details, leading to prohibitive storage costs and slow rendering speeds. We observe that dynamic objects (e.g., vehicles and pedestrians) demand high-fidelity representations to maintain temporal consistency, while static background regions often contain substantial redundancy. Motivated by this, we propose SparseStreet, a general compression framework specifically designed for street scenes. First, we introduce a node-based learnable pruning strategy that systematically removes low-contributing Gaussian primitives while preserving visually critical regions. Second, after the scene representation stabilizes, we apply background compression, further reducing redundancy in static regions. Our method effectively preserves the geometry and appearance of dynamic objects while significantly reducing the total number of Gaussian primitives. Extensive experiments on the Waymo and nuScenes demonstrate that SparseStreet achieves up to 80% compression ratio with minimal quality degradation, enabling resource-efficient, high-fidelity dynamic scene reconstruction. Project website: https://sparsestreet.github.io/.

### [103] [Bootstrap Your Generator: Unpaired Visual Editing with Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03911)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像/视频编辑通常需要大量成对数据，获取代价高且难扩展，尤其是视频。现有方法依赖外部奖励或标注，限制泛化与可扩展性。希望仅用基础生成模型自身知识，在无配对数据下学得高质量编辑能力，并缩小训练与推理差距。

Method: 提出Bootstrap Your Generator（ByG）用于无配对训练的flow matching编辑模型：1）从冻结的基础生成模型中提取指令跟随的语义线索，作为训练监督；2）引入循环一致性约束以保持结构与内容；3）设计梯度路由机制：将下游损失的梯度从干净预测重定向到含噪训练状态，缓解训练-推理不匹配；4）无需外部奖励模型或配对数据即可进行端到端训练。

Result: 在数据稀缺的图像与视频编辑任务上达到SOTA；广泛评测与用户研究显示，对未见域具备良好泛化，且超过使用数百万标注样本的监督基线。消融分析表明梯度路由有效弥合训练-推理差异，从基础模型抽取的语义线索提供了稳健信号。

Conclusion: ByG能在无配对数据与无外部奖励的条件下，高效训练流匹配编辑模型，兼顾编辑遵从与结构保持，具备强泛化，并在少数据场景显著超越大规模监督方法。

Abstract: Modern generative models possess a deep understanding of visual content, yet training them for image editing typically requires massive datasets of paired examples. This limits scalability, especially for video editing where collecting paired data is prohibitively expensive. We propose Bootstrap Your Generator (ByG), a general framework for unpaired training of flow matching editing models. It leverages the base model's knowledge without any external signal. Our approach pairs instruction-following cues extracted from the frozen model with cycle-consistency for structure preservation. To make this tractable, we propose to route gradients from downstream losses over clean predictions to noisy training states. We demonstrate state-of-the-art results on challenging data-scarce image and video editing scenarios. Extensive evaluations and user studies show that our method effectively generalizes to unseen domains and outperforms supervised baselines trained on millions of samples. Analysis reveals that our gradient routing bridges the train-inference gap, and extracting semantic cues from a base model provides a robust training signal that obviates the need for external reward models.

</details>


### [104] [PatchScene: Patch-based Voxel Diffusion for Large-Scale Scene Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03915)
*Qingdong Xu,Jiajun Zhu,Shilin Zhu,Xinjing He,Chao Lu,Huanran Wang,Jiyao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PatchScene是一种面向大规模LiDAR场景补全的扩散模型框架，采用基于patch的体素扩散与置信度引导的时空融合，并提出“环流(Annular-Flow)”扩散策略，从近距向远距逐步传播高保真信息；在SemanticKITTI上达到了SOTA，并能从20 m泛化到50 m无需再训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么依赖全局潜变量、要么采用稠密体素网格，难以在大尺度场景下兼顾几何细节、计算效率与时空一致性，并且对远距离稀疏区域泛化不足。需要一种既能细粒度生成、又能在大范围内保持一致性且可扩展的生成式场景补全方法。

Method: 1) Patch-based Voxel Diffusion：将场景划分为局部3D patch，在每个patch内执行体素扩散以生成精细几何；2) Confidence-guided Spatio-temporal Fusion：在统一生成过程中，利用置信度引导融合重叠patch与相邻帧，保证空间与时间一致性；3) Annular-Flow Diffusion：利用LiDAR从近到远的环形径向密度分布，逐环带把高置信信息从近距传播到远距，实现空间无界的补全。

Result: 在SemanticKITTI基准上所有标准指标均达SOTA，几何精度与时间一致性优于现有方法；同时，使用20 m训练的模型在50 m范围上无需再训练即可良好泛化。

Conclusion: PatchScene通过patch级体素扩散、置信度时空融合与环流扩散三者协同，兼顾细节、全局一致与可扩展性，实现对大尺度、远距LiDAR场景的高质量补全，并展现出强泛化与实际自动驾驶应用潜力。

Abstract: We propose PatchScene, a novel diffusion-based framework for large-scale LiDAR scene completion. Unlike existing methods that rely on global latent representations or dense voxel grids, PatchScene adopts a patch-based voxel diffusion paradigm that explicitly generates fine-grained geometry within localized 3D regions. To ensure coherent reconstruction at both spatial and temporal scales, we introduce a confidence-guided spatio-temporal fusion mechanism that integrates overlapping patches and adjacent frames in a unified generative process. Furthermore, we design an Annular-Flow diffusion strategy that leverages the radial density pattern of LiDAR scans to progressively propagate high-fidelity information from near-range to far-range regions, enabling spatially unbounded scene completion. Extensive experiments on the SemanticKITTI benchmark demonstrate that PatchScene achieves state-of-the-art performance across all standard metrics, surpassing previous approaches in both geometric accuracy and temporal consistency. Remarkably, the model trained on 20 m LiDAR ranges generalizes effectively to 50 m scenes without retraining, highlighting its strong scalability and generalization capability for real-world autonomous driving applications.

### [106] [GARDEN: Gravity-Aligned Reconstruction of Disentangled ENvironments from RGB images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03921)
*Jiahao Sun,Dingkun Wei,Zehong Shen,Hongyu Zhou,Yujun Shen,Liang Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GARDEN将多视角RGB重建重塑为“物理可用”的场景分解：用重力统一坐标→提取物体级刚体网格与6DoF姿态→从背景中剔除重复物体几何，得到可直接用于物理仿真的混合表示，兼顾交互性与逼真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RGB重建产出整体、无显式物理结构的场景：存在全局旋转不定、前景刚体与背景纠缠，导致难以稳定物理交互；以CAD替换求互动虽可行，但检索-替换慢且损失场景特异几何。需要一种既保持外观保真又物理可交互的重建表示。

Method: 提出GARDEN，纯RGB框架，核心是利用“重力”这一通用物理先验：1) 重力-视角对齐，统一坐标系，消除规范任意性；2) 恢复以物体为中心的刚体网格并精确6DoF定位；3) 条件式3D点分类，从背景中移除与已重建物体重复的几何。输出为显式刚体+解耦背景的混合场景表示，可直接驱动物理引擎与渲染。

Result: 在模拟与真实多视角数据上，相比基于检索的基线，提升了：物体放置可靠性、前景-背景解耦质量、渲染到仿真的效率。

Conclusion: 以重力为物理先验的场景因子化可从纯RGB重建中获得结构化、可物理交互的3D表示，兼顾视觉真实与仿真可用性，并优于检索替换式方案。

Abstract: Converting multi-view RGB observations into simulation-ready 3D environments remains challenging because current reconstruction pipelines produce monolithic scene representations without explicit physical structure. They are typically defined up to an arbitrary global rotation and entangle rigid foreground objects with background geometry, which hinders stable physical interaction. Existing solutions often recover interactivity by replacing reconstructed objects with retrieved CAD assets, but this introduces a slow retrieval-and-replacement stage and weakens scene-specific geometric fidelity. We propose GARDEN, an RGB-only framework that reformulates reconstruction as physically-grounded scene factorization and outputs a structured hybrid scene representation. The key idea is to use gravity as a universal physical prior: we first align the reconstruction to a unified Gravity-View frame to resolve gauge ambiguity, then recover object-centric rigid meshes with accurate 6-DoF placement, and finally remove duplicate object geometry from the background through conditional 3D point classification. The resulting representation combines explicit rigid bodies with a decoupled background, enabling direct physics simulation while preserving visual realism. Experiments on both simulated and real multi-view scenes show that GARDEN improves object placement reliability, disentanglement quality, and rendering-simulation efficiency compared with retrieval-based baselines.

### [107] [Adaptive Causal Alignment for High-Confidence Adversarial Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03925)
*Zhiming Luo,Kejia Zhang,Yingxin Lai,Junwei Wu,Juanjuan Weng,Shaozi Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HICAT框架以解决逆向对抗训练中过高置信源于背景过拟合的悖论，通过可学习的背景偏置估计、适应性去偏与前景对齐增强来在利用与抑制上下文之间建立语义平衡，显著缩小鲁棒泛化差距并在多数据集与架构上优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有逆向对抗训练依赖高置信样本稳定鲁棒学习，但高置信常来自对非因果背景相关性的过拟合；视觉上下文既可能是必要先验也可能是伪混淆，盲目抑制会导致特征丢失，因此需要一种能区分并自适应利用/抑制背景的机制。

Method: 提出HICAT（High-Confidence Causally Aligned Training），遵循“测量-去偏-对齐”流程：1）Learnable Background-Bias Estimator（LBBE）学习性地评估每样本背景作为先验或混淆的程度；2）Adaptive Debiasing基于该诊断对logit进行“外科式”校正，抑制由背景驱动的置信；3）Foreground Logit Orthogonal Enhancement（FLOE）基于几何约束使前景与背景表示正交，实施特征解缠并强化前景语义。整体目标是在高置信样本上实现因果对齐与语义平衡。

Result: 在CIFAR-10/100与ImageNet-1K上、针对CNN与ViT等多种架构，HICAT相较匹配基线均有一致提升，并显著缩小鲁棒泛化差距；实验覆盖常规与鲁棒评测场景，显示更稳定的鲁棒学习。

Conclusion: 高置信并非天然可靠，应结合因果诊断与对齐。HICAT通过自适应估计与几何解缠在利用上下文先验与抑制伪相关间取得平衡，提升鲁棒性能并减少泛化差距，可作为逆向对抗训练的统一增强范式。

Abstract: Inverse adversarial training leverages high-confidence predictions to stabilize robust learning, yet we uncover a critical paradox: high confidence often stems from overfitting to non-causal background correlations rather than intrinsic object semantics. Our investigation reveals that visual context functions as a dual-natured signal, serving as either a necessary supportive prior or a spurious confounder. This insight renders existing blind suppression strategies flawed, as they inevitably lead to severe Feature Loss. To resolve this, we propose High-Confidence Causally Aligned Training (HICAT), a unified framework that establishes a Semantic Equilibrium. Operating on a ``Measure-Debias-Align'' pipeline, HICAT integrates a Learnable Background-Bias Estimator (LBBE) to adaptively diagnose context utility. Guided by this diagnosis, an Adaptive Debiasing mechanism performs surgical logit rectification, complemented by a geometrically grounded Foreground Logit Orthogonal Enhancement (FLOE) loss to enforce rigorous feature disentanglement. Extensive experiments on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and ImageNet-1K demonstrate that HICAT consistently improves over matched baselines across diverse architectures (CNNs and ViTs) while significantly reducing the robust generalization gap.

### [110] [Video-Mirai: Autoregressive Video Diffusion Models Need Foresight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03971)
*Yonghao Yu,Lang Huang,Runyi Li,Zerun Wang,Toshihiko Yamasaki*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Video-Mirai：在不改变因果推理/推断的前提下，用“面向未来的表征蒸馏”来弥补自回归视频扩散训练中的表征级规划缺口，从而提升长时一致性与整体质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归视频生成在推断时必须因果（只看过去），但常规训练仅让每个因果状态解释“当前帧/片段”，忽略为未来一致性所需的信息（身份、布局、运动），导致“表征级规划缺口”。需要一种方法在保持因果推断的同时，让训练信号利用未来帧来监督当前表征，使模型学会为未来做计划。

Method: 训练期引入一个“冻结的先见（foresight）编码器”和一个轻量预测头：1) 按因果方式rollout生成完整视频；2) 用非因果的先见编码器读取整个生成序列，得到停止梯度的目标；3) 用预测头将这些未来条件的目标蒸馏到各时间步的因果隐藏状态；4) 仅用未来帧监督表示，不把未来信息喂回生成器输入。推断时丢弃先见编码器与预测头，保持原架构、每步FLOPs与KV-cache不变。

Result: 在VBench 5秒总分从83.8提升至84.6；在超出训练跨度的30秒rollout上，主体一致性由84.9→88.5，背景一致性由90.2→91.9。消融显示“面向未来的目标”是关键；探针表明当前特征对未来帧更可解码。

Conclusion: 在自回归视频模型中，因果性应约束推断而非表征监督。通过训练期的先见蒸馏，可显著提升长时一致性与质量，而无需修改推断时的计算与缓存行为；视觉自回归模型需要“前瞻性”表征。

Abstract: Causal video generators must predict from the past, but they need not learn only from it. In streaming autoregressive video diffusion, each emitted segment becomes a commitment that future segments must preserve. Standard training, however, only asks each causal state to explain the present. This creates what we call a representation-level planning gap: states that fit the current segment may discard identity, layout, and motion information needed for a consistent future. We introduce Video-Mirai, a training-only method that closes this gap without changing causal inference: the generator rolls out causally, a frozen foresight encoder reads the completed rollout non-causally, and a lightweight predictor distills the resulting stopped-gradient targets into causal states. Future frames supervise representations, never generator inputs. At inference, the encoder and predictor are discarded, leaving the original architecture, per-step FLOPs, and KV-cache behavior unchanged. Video-Mirai improves a strong Causal-Forcing baseline on 5-second VBench from 83.8 to 84.6 in terms of Total Score. On 30-second rollouts beyond the training horizon, subject consistency improves from 84.9 to 88.5 and background consistency from 90.2 to 91.9. Ablations identify future-conditioned targets as the key ingredient, and probes show that future frames become more decodable from current features. Causality should constrain inference, not representation supervision. Our study highlights that visual autoregressive models need foresight. Project page: https://y0uroy.github.io/Video-Mirai.

</details>


### [111] [AAD-1: Asymmetric Adversarial Distillation for One-Step Autoregressive Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03972)
*Haobo Li,Yanhong Zeng,Yunhong Lu,Jiapeng Zhu,Hao Ouyang,Qiuyu Wang,Ka Leong Cheng,Yujun Shen,Zhipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AAD-1：用于一步自回归图生视频的非对称对抗蒸馏框架，通过非对称判别器与分阶段训练，缓解动作崩塌与不稳定，VBench上达SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有一步自回归图生视频方法虽然用对抗蒸馏，但常出现动作崩塌（视频静止）与训练不稳定，原因在于判别器与生成器对时空信息对齐、难以检测全局时序失败，且直接对抗训练不稳定。

Method: 两大设计：1) 非对称结构：生成器保持因果（自回归采样能力），判别器双向关注全时空上下文，并输出整段视频的整体真实度分数，以捕捉全局时序错误和长程漂移。2) 分阶段训练：先进行分布匹配预热，学习稳定的一步生成器，使学生分布靠近教师；随后再进行对抗蒸馏，提升时序真实感与动态性。

Result: 在VBench上进行大量实验，AAD-1在一步自回归视频生成的多项指标上达到或超过现有方法，显著减少静帧与运动坍塌。

Conclusion: 通过判别器/生成器的非对称设计与分阶段训练，AAD-1缓解了自回归生成中的全局时序失败与不稳定，实现更稳定且动态真实的一步图生视频，达成SOTA。

Abstract: We present AAD-1, an Asymmetric Adversarial Distillation framework for One-step autoregressive image-to-video generation. State-of-the-art methods adopt adversarial distillation but suffer from motion collapse and training instability, resulting in static videos. AAD-1 addresses these challenges through two key designs in architecture and training strategy. Our key architectural insight is to break the symmetry between generator and discriminator. While the generator remains causal to preserve autoregressive sampling capability, the discriminator attends bidirectionally over the full spatiotemporal context and produces a single holistic realism score for the entire video sequence. This asymmetric design enables the discriminator to effectively detect global temporal failures and long-range drift that cause motion collapse in autoregressive generation. To stabilize training, we introduce a phased strategy that first uses distribution matching to bootstrap a stable one-step generator, providing a warm-up phase that brings the student distribution closer to the teacher before adversarial distillation begins. Extensive experiments on VBench demonstrate that AAD-1 achieves state-of-the-art performance in one-step autoregressive video generation.

</details>


### [112] [Formalizing the Binding Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03976)
*Lianghuan Huang,Yihao Li,Saeed Salehi,Yingshan Chang,Ansh Soni,Konrad P. Kording*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一种信息论探针，量化视觉模型表征中“绑定信息”（哪些特征属于同一对象），并在多种ViT组件与数据集上实证表明：更强的绑定与更好的视觉识别/推理性能相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉场景理解不仅需识别特征，还需知道哪些特征属于同一对象（绑定问题）。尽管ViT能聚合属于同一物体的patch，但现有工作未明确证明模型是否在“特征层面”学习了绑定。实际中ViT常将特征错误归属到相似物体，提示绑定可能是性能瓶颈，需形式化度量。

Method: 以信息论形式化绑定问题，提出探针方法衡量模型表征中的绑定信息；在ViT的不同组件（如CLS全局token与空间token）上进行测量；构建/选用含不同绑定挑战的数据集（特征共享、遮挡、自然图像特征）；比较多种预训练ViT在这些设置下的绑定量与任务表现。

Result: 探针可区分并量化不同ViT及其组件的绑定信息；在具有特征共享与遮挡的场景中，空间token与某些架构变体包含更多可解码的绑定信息；绑定信息的多少与下游识别与推理性能显著正相关。

Conclusion: 绑定信息是强视觉理解与推理的关键要素。ViT内部确实学习到一定的特征绑定，但程度依架构与组件而异；提升与显式利用绑定信息可能改进多物体与复杂场景的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Representations of the world, arguably, contain information about features (e.g. something is blue, something is a circle) but also information about which features are part of the same object (e.g. the circle is blue), which we call binding information. Any system with the ability to understand scenes with multiple objects must be able to solve the binding problem: it needs to know which features belong together. However, despite work showing that Vision Transformers (ViTs) know which patches belong together, it is not known whether current deep learning models learn to exhibit binding information, i.e., for features. We may believe that there is not much binding information, after all misattributing features to wrong objects is a common failure of ViT-based architectures, especially in scenes with objects sharing features. Here we formalize the binding problem with an information-theoretic approach, and introduce a probing method to measure binding information in model representations. We perform experiments on ViTs, measuring binding from different components of the architecture, such as the image summary token [CLS] or the spatial tokens. We use datasets with different binding challenges, such as feature sharing, occlusion, and natural features, while comparing the performance of several pre-trained ViTs. Overall, our research demonstrates binding as a key ingredient to strong visual recognition and reasoning.

</details>


### [113] [NewtPhys: Do Foundation Models Understand Newtonian Physics?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03986)
*Sebastian Cavada,Soumava Paul,Tuan-Hung Vu,Andrei Bursuc,Raoul de Charette*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出NewtPhys，一个真实多视角4D物理标注数据集，用于评估和推动模型的低层牛顿物理理解；在该数据集上系统评测多种VLM/VFM，揭示其低层物理推理局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有物理推理评测多基于合成/半合成场景与VQA，侧重高层事件，缺乏真实视觉复杂度与低层牛顿物理所需的精细标注，难以真正检验模型对力学的理解。

Method: 构建NewtPhys数据集：真实世界多视角图像与基于物理模拟的对齐，提供跨时间的高密度细粒度标注（含3D力、遮挡无关的每像素物理/跟踪/语义/几何量）；据此设计评测协议，系统测试56个VLM（含54开源与2闭源）与10个VFM的低层物理能力。

Result: 实验显示现有VLM与VFM在低层牛顿物理理解上存在显著不足，难以在真实视觉复杂度与精细物理标注场景中可靠推理。

Conclusion: NewtPhys填补从简化合成到真实复杂视觉之间的空白，为物理驱动视觉研究与物理感知评测奠定基准与数据基础，并将促进下一代具物理感知能力的评测与方法发展。

Abstract: Previous work has evaluated physics reasoning in foundation models using synthetic or semi-synthetic scenes and visual question-answering tasks. However, these benchmarks emphasize high-level events and lack the visual fidelity required to assess true low-level Newtonian understanding. We introduce NewtPhys, a 4D physically annotated dataset built from multiview images of real-world scenes with physics-grounded simulations. The dataset provides dense, fine-grained annotations across timesteps -- including 3D forces and amodal per-pixel quantities covering physics, tracking, semantics and geometry -- bridging the gap between simplistic synthetic setups and realistic visual complexity. Using NewtPhys, we systematically evaluate 56 VLMs, including 54 open-weight models and 2 closed-source frontier models, and 10 VFMs and reveal limitations in low-level physics reasoning. Beyond benchmarking, our dataset enables future research in physics-grounded vision and the development of next-generation physics-aware evaluations. Code and datasets are available at https://astra-vision.github.io/NewtPhys.

</details>


### [114] [PixVOD: Pixel-Distributed Direct Visual Odometry and Depth Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03989)
*Shinjeong Kim,Ignacio Alzugaray,Callum Rhodes,Paul H. J. Kelly,Andrew J. Davison*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出在像素级别通过高斯置信传播（GBP）实现分布式视觉里程计与深度估计，并引入“关键帧式锚定”以保持几何稳定，验证了在传感器上进行并行计算的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉系统将含冗余与噪声的2D像素阵列完整传输到下游，通信与能耗低效；而许多计算本可在像素层并行完成。作者希望把部分高层视觉计算前移到焦平面传感-处理器，减轻下游负担并提升输入质量。

Method: - 将视觉里程计与深度估计表述为像素间的分布式推断问题；
- 以每个像素为处理节点，节点基于逐像素光度观测与表面法线先验，使用高斯置信传播（GBP）在像素邻域内交换信息以达成对相机运动与深度的一致估计；
- 设计“关键帧式锚定”机制，调控帧间有效基线，避免优化时的几何不稳定，确保运动与深度的稳健更新；
- 在逼真数据集上评估，模拟焦平面上并行执行。

Result: 实验在现实感数据集上表明：像素级GBP可实现分布式VO与深度估计；关键帧锚定提升了几何稳定性与一致性，证明了在传感器上的并行实现的可行性。

Conclusion: 在传感器像素层进行GBP驱动的分布式里程计与深度估计可减少数据外传、提升系统效率；关键帧锚定是保持稳定优化的关键。该框架为面向焦平面计算的下一代视觉系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Images composed of 2D pixel arrays are the standard input to computer vision algorithms, yet many underlying computations can be distributed across pixels. Transmitting raw, redundant, and noisy pixel data off the sensor remains inefficient, motivating a shift toward focal-plane sensor-processors that perform a significant part of the computation directly within each pixel. We envision pixels synthesizing higher-level signals locally, reducing downstream load, and providing richer inputs for higher-level vision tasks.
  We propose a fully parallelizable form of visual odometry and depth estimation across pixels, where sensor-processors exchange information through Gaussian Belief Propagation (GBP) to achieve consensus about camera motion and infer depth from per-pixel photometric observations and a surface normal prior. To maintain geometric stability during optimization, we introduce a keyframe-like anchoring mechanism that regulates the effective baseline between frames, enabling consistent motion and depth updates. Our method is evaluated on realistic datasets, demonstrating the feasibility of GBP-based pixel-level distributed odometry and depth estimation with keyframe anchoring on-sensor. Project Page: https://www.shinjeongkim.com/pixvod/

</details>


### [115] [Exploring Easy Boosts for Lidar Semantic Scene Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03992)
*Tetiana Martyniuk,Jonathan Seele,Alexandre Boulch,Gilles Puy,Renaud Marlet,Raoul de Charette*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出无需复杂模型改造的“白嫖式”策略即可显著提升激光雷达语义场景补全（SSC）：给输入点云添加由现成分割器生成的语义伪标签，以及加入可见性（区分空与未知）。两者带来显著mIoU提升，使老模型在增强后可匹配甚至超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前提升SSC性能多依赖复杂架构设计与训练技巧，成本高、可复用性差。作者观察到输入先验（语义与可见性）可能是关键瓶颈，若能以低成本注入高质量先验，是否能让现有甚至旧模型显著受益？

Method: 1) 使用开箱即用的点云/多模态分割器为输入激光雷达点添加语义伪标签，并将其作为额外通道或特征输入现有SSC网络。2) 引入可见性先验，显式区分体素中的“空”和“未知”区域，减少歧义。3) 通过与“oracle”语义先验（理想高质量标签）对比，量化先验质量对mIoU的贡献。4) 在多种现有SSC架构上做消融与对比。

Result: - 高质量语义先验是mIoU提升的主因；可见性先验提供次级但稳定的收益。- 简单增强后，多种旧架构与最新SOTA持平或超越。- 证明性能瓶颈更多在输入先验而非模型复杂度。

Conclusion: 在SSC中，注入高质量语义与可见性先验是“性价比极高”的途径，无需改动模型即可显著增益；社区应更重视输入先验与数据层增强。代码已开源，便于复现与应用。

Abstract: This paper investigates "free lunch" strategies to boost the performance of lidar semantic scene completion (SSC) without requiring complex architectural redesigns. We first demonstrate that endowing input point clouds with semantic pseudo-labels from off-the-shelf segmentors significantly improves the performance of existing architectures. By evaluating these models against an oracle, we establish that high-quality semantic priors are a primary driver of mIoU gains. Furthermore, we equip the input lidar scan with visibility information that distinguishes between empty and unknown spaces, which provides a secondary performance boost across the tested architectures. Using these simple enhancements, we observe that older models remain competitive with state-of-the-art systems, and can even outperform them. Our code is available at https://github.com/astra-vision/SSC-Priors.

</details>


### [116] [SimuScene: Simulation-Ready Compositional 3D Scene Reconstruction from a Single Image](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03994)
*Inhee Lee,Sangwon Baik,Sungjoo Kim,Hyeonwoo Kim,Hyunsoo Cha,Hanbyul Joo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SimuScene将物理引擎融入单张图像到可仿真3D场景重建流程，通过诊断式仿真产生可量化纠正信号，联合形状与布局迭代修正，生成稳定、无互穿、可交互的组合场景，显著提升物理稳定性与几何对齐，并在人形与机械臂任务中验证有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单图重建的逐物体提举方法组合后常出现互穿、悬空、下陷，导致物理仿真中场景坍塌；既有物理感知方法多做事后布局修正，无法根治底层几何误差。需要一种把物理反馈前置到重建过程、同时修正形状与布局的方案。

Method: 提出SimuScene：在生成过程中把物理引擎作为诊断工具。对重建对象在重力下进行快速仿真，量化渗透与支撑失败，转化为纠正信号，驱动沿重力轴的形状拉伸与遮挡外（amodal）形状重采样，并联动布局优化，形成物理知情的闭环反馈，得到稳定的组合3D场景。

Result: 在物理稳定性与几何对齐基准上达到SOTA；重建场景可直接用于人形体控制与机械臂抓取/操作，展现更高成功率与稳定性。

Conclusion: 将物理诊断前置并与形状与布局联合优化，可有效抑制误差累积，获得仿真就绪的稳定组合场景；物理在环的重建范式优于事后清理。

Abstract: Reconstructing interactive, simulation-ready 3D scenes from a single image is a critical bottleneck for robotic manipulation. While recent single-image lifters recover plausible per-object shapes, composing them yields scenes that collapse under physical simulation due to interpenetrating, hovering, or sinking objects. Existing physics-aware methods address this strictly as a post-hoc layout correction, leaving the underlying geometric errors unresolved. To address this, we introduce SimuScene, a compositional 3D reconstruction pipeline that puts physics in the loop of shape and layout estimation. Rather than using physics merely for layout cleanup, we utilize the physics engine as a diagnostic measurement tool during the generative process itself. By diagnostically simulating reconstructed objects under gravity, we convert penetration and support failures into quantitative correction signals that drive gravity-axis stretching and amodal shape resampling. This physics-informed feedback loop mitigates accumulated reconstruction errors and produces a stable, simulation-ready compositional 3D scene. Extensive experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance on physical stability and geometric alignment benchmarks. We further highlight SimuScene's utility by deploying reconstructed environments in humanoid control and robot-arm manipulation tasks.

</details>
